fruit_classifier.py
```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = tf.keras.utils.to_categorical(labels, num_classes=len(label_to_int))
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```

fruit_classifier.py
```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = tf.keras.utils.to_categorical(labels, num_classes=len(label_to_int))
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```

streamlit_app.py
```python
'''
This module contains the StreamlitApp class for creating the GUI for the fruit freshness
classification application.
'''
import streamlit as st
from fruit_classifier import FruitClassifier
from PIL import Image
import numpy as np
class StreamlitApp:
    def __init__(self):
        self.classifier = FruitClassifier()
    def upload_image(self):
        # Allow users to upload fruit images
        uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Choose a fruit image...", type=["jpg", "jpeg", "png"])
        if uploaded_file is not None:
            image = Image.open(uploaded_file)
            st.image(image, caption='Uploaded Image.', use_column_width=True)
            return image
        return None
    def display_results(self, prediction):
        # Display classification results and predictions
        st.write("Prediction Results:")
        st.write(f"Freshness Class: {np.argmax(prediction)}")
        st.write(f"Remaining Days Before Expiry: {prediction[0][2]} days")  # Assuming index 2 for days
    def run(self):
        st.title("Fruit Freshness Classification")
        image = self.upload_image()
        if image is not None:
            prediction = self.classifier.predict(image)
            self.display_results(prediction)
```

```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = np.array(labels)
        labels = np.eye(len(label_to_int))[labels]
        return np.array(images), labels
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```

import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os

    def __init__(self):

        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):

                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])

        labels = np.eye(len(label_to_int))[labels]

            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)

fruit_classifier.py
```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = tf.keras.utils.to_categorical(labels, num_classes=len(label_to_int))
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```

streamlit_app.py
```python
'''
This module contains the StreamlitApp class for creating the GUI for the fruit freshness
classification application.
'''
import streamlit as st
from fruit_classifier import FruitClassifier
from PIL import Image
import numpy as np
class StreamlitApp:
    def __init__(self):
        self.classifier = FruitClassifier()
    def upload_image(self):
        # Allow users to upload fruit images
        uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Choose a fruit image...", type=["jpg", "jpeg", "png"])
        if uploaded_file is not None:
            image = Image.open(uploaded_file)
            st.image(image, caption='Uploaded Image.', use_column_width=True)
            return image
        return None
    def display_results(self, prediction):
        # Display classification results and predictions
        st.write("Prediction Results:")
        st.write(f"Freshness Class: {np.argmax(prediction)}")
        st.write(f"Remaining Days Before Expiry: {prediction[0][2]} days")  # Assuming index 2 for days
    def run(self):
        st.title("Fruit Freshness Classification")
        image = self.upload_image()
        if image is not None:
            prediction = self.classifier.predict(image)
            self.display_results(prediction)
```

fruit_classifier.py
```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = tf.keras.utils.to_categorical(labels, num_classes=len(label_to_int))
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```
streamlit_app.py
```python
'''
This module contains the StreamlitApp class for creating the GUI for the fruit freshness
classification application.
'''
import streamlit as st
from fruit_classifier import FruitClassifier
from PIL import Image
import numpy as np
class StreamlitApp:
    def __init__(self):
        self.classifier = FruitClassifier()
    def upload_image(self):
        # Allow users to upload fruit images
        uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Choose a fruit image...", type=["jpg", "jpeg", "png"])
        if uploaded_file is not None:
            image = Image.open(uploaded_file)
            st.image(image, caption='Uploaded Image.', use_column_width=True)
            return image
        return None
    def display_results(self, prediction):
        # Display classification results and predictions
        st.write("Prediction Results:")
        st.write(f"Freshness Class: {np.argmax(prediction)}")
        st.write(f"Remaining Days Before Expiry: {prediction[0][2]} days")  # Assuming index 2 for days
    def run(self):
        st.title("Fruit Freshness Classification")
        image = self.upload_image()
        if image is not None:
            prediction = self.classifier.predict(image)
            self.display_results(prediction)
```

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program to build a deep learning model using CNN to classify fruit freshness, predict remaining days before expiry, and create a Streamlit GUI for uploading fruit images, displaying classification results and predictions.".

fruit_classifier.py
```python
'''
This module contains the FruitClassifier class for building and training a CNN model
to classify fruit freshness and predict remaining days before expiry.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image
import os
class FruitClassifier:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def load_data(self, data_path):
        # Load and preprocess image data
        images = []
        labels = []
        label_to_int = {label: idx for idx, label in enumerate(os.listdir(data_path))}
        for label in os.listdir(data_path):
            label_path = os.path.join(data_path, label)
            for image_file in os.listdir(label_path):
                image_path = os.path.join(label_path, image_file)
                image = Image.open(image_path).resize((100, 100))
                image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
                images.append(image_array)
                labels.append(label_to_int[label])
        # Convert labels to one-hot encoding
        labels = tf.keras.utils.to_categorical(labels, num_classes=len(label_to_int))
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
    def build_model(self):
        # Construct the CNN architecture
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(100, 100, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(128, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(3, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 3 classes for freshness
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train_model(self, train_data, train_labels):
        # Train the CNN model
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=10)
    def predict(self, image):
        # Predict freshness and remaining days before expiry
        image = image.resize((100, 100))
        image_array = np.array(image) / 255.0
        image_array = np.expand_dims(image_array, axis=0)
        prediction = self.model.predict(image_array)
        return prediction
```

streamlit_app.py
```python
'''
This module contains the StreamlitApp class for creating the GUI for the fruit freshness
classification application.
'''
import streamlit as st
from fruit_classifier import FruitClassifier
from PIL import Image
import numpy as np
class StreamlitApp:
    def __init__(self):
        self.classifier = FruitClassifier()
    def upload_image(self):
        # Allow users to upload fruit images
        uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Choose a fruit image...", type=["jpg", "jpeg", "png"])
        if uploaded_file is not None:
            image = Image.open(uploaded_file)
            st.image(image, caption='Uploaded Image.', use_column_width=True)
            return image
        return None
    def display_results(self, prediction):
        # Display classification results and predictions
        st.write("Prediction Results:")
        st.write(f"Freshness Class: {np.argmax(prediction)}")
        st.write(f"Remaining Days Before Expiry: {prediction[0][2]} days")  # Assuming index 2 for days
    def run(self):
        st.title("Fruit Freshness Classification")
        image = self.upload_image()
        if image is not None:
            prediction = self.classifier.predict(image)
            self.display_results(prediction)
```

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

# Fruit Freshness Classification Application User Manual

Welcome to the Fruit Freshness Classification Application! This application is designed to classify fruit freshness and predict the remaining days before expiry using a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) deep learning model. You can easily interact with the application through a user-friendly Streamlit GUI by uploading fruit images and viewing the classification results and predictions.

## Main Functions

1. **Upload Fruit Images**: Users can upload images of fruits for classification.
2. **Display Classification Results**: The application displays the freshness class and the remaining days before expiry based on the uploaded image.
3. **Predict Remaining Days Before Expiry**: The deep learning model predicts the remaining days before the fruit expires.

## Installation

To run the Fruit Freshness Classification Application, make sure you have the required dependencies installed in your Python environment. You can install the dependencies by running the following command:

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

## How to Use

1. **Run the Application**:
   - Open a terminal window.
   - Navigate to the directory where the `main.py` file is located.
   - Run the following command:
     ```bash
     python main.py
     ```
2. **Interact with the GUI**:
   - Once the application is running, a web browser window will open automatically.
   - You will see the title "Fruit Freshness Classification" displayed.
   - Click on the "Choose a fruit image..." button to upload an image of a fruit for classification.
   - After uploading the image, the application will display the uploaded image along with the classification results and predictions.

## Note

- The application assumes 3 classes for freshness classification.
- The prediction for the remaining days before expiry is based on the model's output.

 # Fruit Freshness Classification Application User Manual

Welcome to the Fruit Freshness Classification Application! This application is designed to classify fruit freshness and predict the remaining days before expiry using a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) deep learning model. You can easily interact with the application through a user-friendly Streamlit GUI by uploading fruit images and viewing the classification results and predictions.

## Main Functions

1. **Upload Fruit Images**: Users can upload images of fruits for classification.
2. **Display Classification Results**: The application displays the freshness class and the remaining days before expiry based on the uploaded image.
3. **Predict Remaining Days Before Expiry**: The deep learning model predicts the remaining days before the fruit expires.

## Installation

To run the Fruit Freshness Classification Application, make sure you have the required dependencies installed in your Python environment. You can install the dependencies by running the following command:

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

## How to Use

1. **Run the Application**:
   - Open a terminal window.
   - Navigate to the directory where the `main.py` file is located.
   - Run the following command:
     ```bash
     python main.py
     ```
2. **Interact with the GUI**:
   - Once the application is running, a web browser window will open automatically.
   - You will see the title "Fruit Freshness Classification" displayed.
   - Click on the "Choose a fruit image..." button to upload an image of a fruit for classification.
   - After uploading the image, the application will display the uploaded image along with the classification results and predictions.

## Note

- The application assumes 3 classes for freshness classification.
- The prediction for the remaining days before expiry is based on the model's output.

Enjoy using the Fruit Freshness Classification Application! If you have any questions or feedback, feel free to reach out to us.
